=== Function: g ===

Code: {
        bytes memory data = hex"1234567890abcdef1234567890abcdef1234567890abcdef1234567890abcdef";
        uint8 result;
        assembly {
            // data pointer is at data + 0x20 (skip length field)
            let ptr := add(data, 0x20)
            // Load first 32 bytes
            let word := mload(ptr)
            // Extract first byte (0x12) - shift right by 248 bits to get leftmost byte
            result := shr(248, word)
        }
        return result;
    }

Code: assembly {

            let ptr := add(data, 0x20)
            // Load first 32 bytes
            let word := mload(ptr)
            // Extract first byte (0x12) - shift right by 248 bits to get leftmost byte
            result := shr(248, word)

=== Function: readFirstByte ===

Code: {
        // Guard: ensure data is non-empty before reading
        require(data.length > 0, "data is empty"); // prevent reading from empty data

        assembly {
            // data pointer is at data + 0x20 (skip length field)
            let ptr := add(data, 0x20)
            // Load first 32 bytes
            let word := mload(ptr)
            // Extract first byte (leftmost) by shifting right 248 bits
            result := shr(248, word)
        }
    }

=== Function: readMiddleByte ===

Code: {
        bytes memory data = hex"123456";
        
        assembly {
            let ptr := add(data, 0x21) // skip length + first byte
            let word := mload(ptr)
            result := shr(248, word)
        }
    }
